	id = MEX.test
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event MEX.test"}
	title = MEX.test.t
	desc = MEX.test.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_last_common_thread

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = MEX.test.a
	}
}

country_event = { # Month + 1 hour tick
	id = MEX.1
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event MEX.1"
		for_each_loop = {
			array = MEX_econ_region_array

			MEX_econ_debt_update_monthly = yes
		}

		# Month check yearly calculations (debt limit, goals)
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { MEX_month_num = 0 } # January
			}
			MEX_econ_debt_limit_reload = yes
			MEX_econ_goal_check_yearly = yes
		}
		MEX_econ_refresh_all_graphs_monthly = yes
	}
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
}

country_event = { # Lopez Mateos gives large authority to ordaz and lozano protests
	id = MEX_Mateos.23
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event MEX_Mateos.23"}
	title = MEX_Mateos.23.t
	desc = MEX_Mateos.23.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_lozano_angry

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #LM decides to stick to his choice
		name = MEX_Mateos.23.a
		MEX_SB_low_raise_Ordaz = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_Mateos.23.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			MEX_PRI_increase_loyalty_businessmen_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_increase_loyalty_workers_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_increase_loyalty_peasants_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_increase_loyalty_dfs_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_increase_loyalty_intellectuals_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_increase_loyalty_officials_low = yes
			set_country_flag = ordaz_stewardship
			set_variable = { MEX_el_tapado_ordaz_stewardship_frame_var = 3 }
			set_variable = { MEX_el_tapado_lozano_stewardship_frame_var = 2 }
		}
	}
	option = { #LM waffles and changes his mind, is punished for it by the PRI
		name = MEX_Mateos.23.b
		MEX_SB_low_raise_Lozano = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_Mateos.23.tt.1
		hidden_effect = {
			MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_businessmen_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_workers_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_peasants_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_dfs_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_intellectuals_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_officials_low = yes
			set_country_flag = lozano_stewardship
			set_variable = { MEX_el_tapado_ordaz_stewardship_frame_var = 2 }
			set_variable = { MEX_el_tapado_lozano_stewardship_frame_var = 3 }
		}
	}
}

## Internal Politics - Policy Dilemmas ##
country_event = { # Compromise on tariffs
	id = MEX_Mateos.25
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event MEX_Mateos.25"}
	title = MEX_Mateos.25.t
	desc = MEX_Mateos.25.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_compromise_on_tariffs

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Yes
		name = MEX_Mateos.25.a
		MEX_SB_low_raise_Ordaz = yes
		add_to_array = {
			array = GBP_ordaz_array
			value = 5
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = MEX_USA_proposal_value
			value = 1
			tooltip = MEX_pro_america1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_businessmen_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_workers_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_peasants_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_dfs_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_intellectuals_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_officials_low = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # No
		name = MEX_Mateos.25.b
		add_to_variable = {
			var = MEX_USA_proposal_value
			value = -1
			tooltip = MEX_pro_mexico1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_Mateos.25.tt.1
		hidden_effect = {
			MEX_PRI_increase_loyalty_businessmen_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_increase_loyalty_workers_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_increase_loyalty_peasants_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_increase_loyalty_dfs_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_increase_loyalty_intellectuals_low = yes
			MEX_PRI_increase_loyalty_officials_low = yes
		}
	}
}

		}

		MEX_SB_low_raise_Lozano = yes

		}

		MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_intellectuals_med = yes
		MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_businessmen_med = yes
		add_to_variable = {
			var = MEX_USA_proposal_value
			value = 1
			tooltip = MEX_pro_america1
		}
		MEX_SB_low_raise_Ordaz = yes
		add_to_array = {
			array = GBP_ordaz_array
			value = 6
		}
	}
}

	id = MEX_Mateos.28
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event MEX_Mateos.28"}
	title = MEX_Mateos.28.t
	desc = MEX_Mateos.28.desc

	option = { #Reduce barriers for american autos

		MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_workers_low = yes

	desc = MEX_Mateos.98.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_jp_agreement

	option = { # Will Japan Back Mexico In The Olympics?
		name = MEX_Mateos.98.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_Mateos.98.tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { MEX_JAP_proposal_value > 3 }
			}
			country_event = { id = MEX_Mateos.99 days = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { MEX_JAP_proposal_value > 1 }
			}
			country_event = { id = MEX_Mateos.102 days = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { MEX_JAP_proposal_value < 2 }
			}
			country_event = { id = MEX_Mateos.108 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #olachea buys jets and helicopter purchase
	id = MEX_Flavor.44
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event MEX_Flavor.44" }
	title = MEX_Flavor.44.t
	desc = MEX_Flavor.44.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_olachea

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Just jets
		name = MEX_Flavor.44.a
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.02 }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = jet_interceptor_equipment_1
			amount = 40
			producer = USA
		}
		air_experience = 10
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = MEX_Flavor.45 days = 352 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Jets and helicopters
		name = MEX_Flavor.44.b
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.035 }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = jet_interceptor_equipment_1
			amount = 40
			producer = USA
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = attack_helicopter_equipment_1
			amount = 20
			producer = USA
		}
		air_experience = 20
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = air_assault_tech
			bonus = 0.5
			uses = 1
			category = air_assault_tech
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = MEX_Flavor.45 days = 352 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Mateos has a stroke looking at dirty war code
	id = MEX_Olympics.13
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event MEX_Olympics.13"}
	title = MEX_Olympics.13.t
	desc = MEX_Olympics.13.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_night_sky

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = MEX_Olympics.13.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Diagnosis is very bad
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = MEX_SB_STRESS_sl
						value = 70
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = MEX_Olympics.14 days = 5 }
			}
			else = { # Diagnosis is slightly positive but still bad
				country_event = { id = MEX_Olympics.15 days = 5 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Lopez Mateos informed of kabuki effect
	id = MEX_Kabuki.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event MEX_Kabuki.1"}
	title = MEX_Kabuki.1.t
	desc = MEX_Kabuki.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_mateos_1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = MEX_Kabuki.1.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_Kabuki_Effect_Change_event_1_tt
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = kabuki_page_turned }
			set_variable = { MEX_kabuki_turn_background_var = 3 }
		}
		set_variable = { MEX_el_tapado_background_var = 3 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.5 }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		BFM_decrease_japan_influence_high = yes
		MEX_SB_high_decrease_Lozano = yes
		add_to_array = {
			array = GBP_lozano_kabuki_array
			value = 1
		}
		MEX_SB_mid_decrease_Ordaz = yes
		add_to_array = {
			array = GBP_ordaz_kabuki_array
			value = 1
		}
		MEX_SB_mid_raise_LAN = yes
		add_to_array = {
			array = GBP_lan_kabuki_array
			value = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { MEX_Madrazo_gbp > 0 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = madrazo_unites }
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = MEX_Mateos.206 days = 1 }
		}
		set_political_power = 200
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = MEX_The_Kabuki_Effect
			add_to_array = { MEX_the_kabuki_effect_effects_array = 0 }
			add_to_array = { MEX_the_kabuki_effect_effects_array = 0.15 }
			add_to_array = { MEX_the_kabuki_effect_effects_array = -2 }
			add_to_array = { MEX_the_kabuki_effect_effects_array = -0.5 }
			add_to_array = { MEX_the_kabuki_effect_effects_array = -0.5 }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = MEX_the_kabuki_effect_effects }
			country_event = { id = MEX_Flavor.14 days = 16 }
			country_event = { id = MEX_Nava.1 days = 46 }
			country_event = { id = MEX_Kabuki.2 days = 2 }
			MEX = { news_event = { id = MEX_News.2 hours = 2 } }
			set_country_flag = kabuki_effect_tree_flag
			clr_country_flag = mateos_fakeout_flag
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #LM picks a economic plan
	id = MEX_Kabuki.10
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event MEX_Kabuki.10"}
	title = MEX_Kabuki.10.t
	desc = MEX_Kabuki.10.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_lm_choose_a_plan

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Rally the Party
		name = MEX_Kabuki.10.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MEX_Lozano_gbp < MEX_Ordaz_gbp }
				check_variable = { MEX_Lozano_gbp = MEX_Ordaz_gbp }
				check_variable = { MEX_Lozano_gbp < MEX_Madrazo_gbp }
				check_variable = { MEX_Lozano_gbp = MEX_Madrazo_gbp }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_Kabuki_crisis_evolves_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { MEX_Lozano_gbp < MEX_Ordaz_gbp }
					check_variable = { MEX_Lozano_gbp < MEX_Madrazo_gbp }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_Kabuki.10.tt2
		}
		else_if = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_Kabuki.10.tt3
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = MEX_Kabuki.11
				days = 1
			}
			MEX_kabuki_start_up = yes
			set_country_flag = MEX_kabuki_crisis_builds_up_image
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_Kabuki.10.tt
		complete_national_focus = MEX_rallying_the_party
		MEX_SB_low_raise_Ordaz = yes
		add_to_array = {
			array = GBP_ordaz_kabuki_array
			value = 2
		}
		MEX_SB_low_raise_LAN = yes
		add_to_array = {
			array = GBP_lan_kabuki_array
			value = 2
		}
	}
	option = { #Technocratic Counter
		name = MEX_Kabuki.10.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MEX_Lozano_gbp > MEX_Ordaz_gbp }
				check_variable = { MEX_Lozano_gbp = MEX_Ordaz_gbp }
			}
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MEX_Lozano_gbp > MEX_Madrazo_gbp }
				check_variable = { MEX_Lozano_gbp = MEX_Madrazo_gbp }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_Kabuki_crisis_evolves_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { MEX_Lozano_gbp > MEX_Ordaz_gbp }
				check_variable = { MEX_Lozano_gbp > MEX_Madrazo_gbp }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_Kabuki.10.tt4
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_Kabuki.10.tt5
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = MEX_Kabuki.12
				days = 1
			}
			MEX_kabuki_start_up = yes
			set_country_flag = MEX_kabuki_crisis_builds_up_image
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_Kabuki.10.tt
		complete_national_focus = MEX_the_technocratic_counter
		MEX_SB_low_raise_Lozano = yes
		add_to_array = {
			array = GBP_lozano_kabuki_array
			value = 2
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #	Mateos Weighs the Successors
	id = MEX_Nava.28
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event MEX_Nava.28"}
	title = MEX_Nava.28.t
	desc = MEX_Nava.28.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_lozano_kabuki

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = MEX_Nava.28.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_Kabuki_crisis_evolves_tt
		clr_country_flag = MEX_Succession_flag
		set_country_flag = MEX_kabuki_crisis_ends_image
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_Nava.28.tt
		if = {
			limit = { #Ordaz Victory
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { MEX_Ordaz_gbp > MEX_Lozano_gbp }
							check_variable = { MEX_Ordaz_gbp = MEX_Lozano_gbp }
						}
						OR = {
							check_variable = { MEX_Ordaz_gbp > MEX_Madrazo_gbp }
							check_variable = { MEX_Ordaz_gbp = MEX_Madrazo_gbp }
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = MEX_PATH
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_PATH
						option = MEX_PATH_ORDAZ
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = MEX_Mateos.19 days = 1 } }
		}
		else_if = { #Salinas Victory
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { MEX_Lozano_gbp > MEX_Ordaz_gbp }
						OR = {
							check_variable = { MEX_Lozano_gbp > MEX_Madrazo_gbp }
							check_variable = { MEX_Lozano_gbp = MEX_Madrazo_gbp }
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = MEX_PATH
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_PATH
						option = MEX_PATH_LOZANO
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = MEX_Mateos.17 days = 1 } }
		}
		else = { #Madrazo Victory
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = MEX_Mateos.18 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Trujillo killed John Marston-style
	id = MEX_Trujillo_Conspiracy.11
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event MEX_Trujillo_Conspiracy.1"}
	title = MEX_Trujillo_Conspiracy.11.t
	desc = MEX_Trujillo_Conspiracy.11.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_DOM_trujillo

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = MEX_Trujillo_Conspiracy.11.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # High MEX/USA intel and cooperation
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { global.PP_spy_strength_CAL > 69 }
							check_variable = { MEX.PP_mexican_american_cooperation > 15 }
							NOT = {
								OR = {
									has_game_rule = {
										rule = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME
										option = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME_BAL_CEASEFIRE
									}
									has_game_rule = {
										rule = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME
										option = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME_BAL_VICTORY
									}
								}
							}
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME
							option = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME_DOM_AGREEMENT
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME
							option = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME_RAM_VICTORY
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = MEX_Trujillo_Conspiracy.12
					hours = 6
				}
			}
			else = { # Not enough intel or cooperation
				country_event = {
					id = MEX_Trujillo_Conspiracy.14
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		set_temp_variable = { ceasefire_tension_temp = 10 }
		TNO_PPI_decrease_ceasefire_tension_substantial = yes

			set_country_flag = MEX_Trujillo_Conspiracy_34_happened
			ZZZ = { activate_mission = ZZZ_PPI_DOM_CAL_Negotiations }
			USA = {
				remove_mission = USA_PPI_ceasefire_ends
				clr_country_flag = USA_PP_ceasefire_legion
				clr_country_flag = USA_PP_ceasefire_balaguer
				set_country_flag = USA_PP_ceasefire_golden_ending
				country_event = { id = USA_Trujillo_Conspiracy.10 }
			}
			IBR = { country_event = { id = HIS_PP_ceasefire.22 } }
			GER = { country_event = { id = HIS_PP_ceasefire.25 } }
			MEX = { country_event = { id = MEX_Puerto_Plata.12 hours = 16} }
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = { id = hispaniola_news.7 hours = 8 } # Trujillo bros, it's over.
			}
			319 = { set_state_name = STATE_319_CAL }
			set_province_name = {
				id = 7660
				name = VICTORY_POINTS_7660_CAL
			}
			DOM = {
				set_politics = { ruling_party = despotism }
				set_popularities = {
					fascism = 15
					despotism = 25
					paternalism = 37
					liberalism = 10
					socialist = 13
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = DOM_Jose_Rene_Roman
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						desc = "POLITICS_JOSE_RENE_ROMAN_DESC"
						expire = "1999.1.1"
						ideology = despotism_interim_government_subtype
						traits = { }
						id = -1
					}
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = despotism
					name = DOM_despotism_party
					long_name = DOM_despotism_party_long
				}
				add_ideas = {
					DOM_The_Dominican_Revolution_0
					DOM_The_Living_Ghost
				}
				remove_ideas = {
					DOM_ceasefire_Mobilization
					DOM_ceasefire_New_State
					IBR_Army_Engineers
					DOM_BSI_detachment
					GER_Wehrmacht_Technicians
					Generic_receiving_intel
				}
				econ_leave_sphere = yes
				set_stability = 0.3
				set_war_support = 0.3
			}
			MEX = { set_variable = { trade_opinion_embargo@DOM = 0 } }
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = DOM
				modifier = TNO_embargo_100
			}
			DOM = {
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = MEX modifier = TNO_embargoed_us_100 }
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = CUB modifier = DOM_caribbean_tension }
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = WIN modifier = DOM_caribbean_tension }
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = MEX modifier = DOM_caribbean_tension }
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = VEN modifier = DOM_caribbean_tension }
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = USA_DOM_hostile_diplomacy }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = MEX modifier = DOM_supported_anti_trujillo_coup }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = DOM_supported_anti_trujillo_coup }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = CUB modifier = DOM_supported_anti_trujillo_coup }
			}
			CUB = { remove_opinion_modifier = { target = DOM modifier = DOM_caribbean_tension } }
			WIN = { remove_opinion_modifier = { target = DOM modifier = DOM_caribbean_tension } }
			MEX = { remove_opinion_modifier = { target = DOM modifier = DOM_caribbean_tension } }
			VEN = { remove_opinion_modifier = { target = DOM modifier = DOM_caribbean_tension } }
			BRA = { remove_opinion_modifier = { target = DOM modifier = DOM_caribbean_tension } }
			USA = { remove_opinion_modifier = { target = DOM modifier = USA_DOM_hostile_diplomacy } }
		}
	}

	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = MEX_mega_melchorocampo.5.t
	desc = MEX_mega_melchorocampo.5.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_mateos_reading
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event MEX_mega_melchorocampo.5"
	}
	option = {
		name = MEX_mega_melchorocampo.5.a

		set_temp_variable = { temp_region = 8 }
		MEX_econ_region_base_stimulation_percent_increase_med = yes
		BFM_increase_usa_influence_med = yes
		BFM_increase_japan_influence_high = yes
		MEX_PRI_decrease_loyalty_businessmen_med = yes
		TNO_worsen_trade_laws_policy_effectiveness_high = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = MEX_mega_melchorocampo.5.b

		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = MEX_michoacan_income_natspirit
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_econ_project_improve_quintana_roo_2
		MEX_PRI_increase_power_businessmen_low = yes
		MEX_PRI_increase_loyalty_businessmen_low = yes
		MEX_decrease_usa_business_opinion_low = yes
		MEX_decrease_jap_business_opinion_low = yes
	}
}

# Regional Debt Crisis passes mission time, decision between intervention and neglect
country_event = {
	id = MEX_debt_crisis.1
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event MEX_debt_crisis.1"
	}
	title = MEX_debt_crisis.1.t
	desc = MEX_debt_crisis.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_bracero_program

	# Intervention
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = MEX_debt_crisis_can_intervene
		}
		name = MEX_debt_crisis_response_intervene
		set_temp_variable = { temp_region = 1 }

		MEX_econ_debt_crisis_intervene = yes
	}

	# Neglect
	option = {
		name = MEX_debt_crisis_response_neglect
		set_temp_variable = { temp_region = 1 }

		MEX_econ_debt_crisis_neglect = yes
	}
}

	# Neglect
	option = {
		name = MEX_debt_crisis_response_neglect
		set_temp_variable = { temp_region = 10 }

		MEX_econ_debt_crisis_neglect = yes
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		set_country_flag = MEX_git_crisis_b
	}

		name = MEX_git_crisis.1.c

	}

country_event = {
	id = MEX_git_crisis.2
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = MEX_git_crisis.2.t
	desc = MEX_git_crisis_end
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = git_crisis_active
	}

	option = { # delete red-italy-branch
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = MEX_git_crisis_a
		}
		name = MEX_git_crisis.2.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_git_crisis.2.a.tt
		clr_country_flag = git_crisis_active
		clr_country_flag = MEX_git_crisis_a
		clr_country_flag = MEX_git_crisis_b
		clr_country_flag = MEX_git_crisis_c
	}
	option = { # delete all branches
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = MEX_git_crisis_b
		}
		name = MEX_git_crisis.2.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_git_crisis.2.b.tt
		clr_country_flag = git_crisis_active
		clr_country_flag = MEX_git_crisis_a
		clr_country_flag = MEX_git_crisis_b
		clr_country_flag = MEX_git_crisis_c
	}
	option = { # retreat to church
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MEX_git_crisis_a }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MEX_git_crisis_b }
			}
		}
		name = MEX_git_crisis.2.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_git_crisis.2.c.tt
		clr_country_flag = git_crisis_active
		clr_country_flag = MEX_git_crisis_a
		clr_country_flag = MEX_git_crisis_b
		clr_country_flag = MEX_git_crisis_c
	}
}
